Business Domain Mid-range Management Plan (FY2016-FY2018) “Together We Innovate GEMBA Worldwide: Growth Toward Our 100th Anniversary (2021) and Beyond” Implementation of ● Growth strategies based on innovation management policy Enhancing the trust placed in us ● Growth strategies of existing businesses → Contributing ● Structural reforms designed to reinforce the business foundation to society by society ● Paying attention to ESG → Further growth Management Strategy Values, basic attitudes and patterns of behavior to be passed on to future generations. 1. To further cultivate the forward-looking corporate climate and the corporate culture of continuously taking on challenges, we will thoroughly ensure group-wide practice of five Gen principles, i.e., Gemba (workpace), Genbutsu (actual things), Genjitsu (reality), Genten (the origin) and Kenzaika (making evident). The KOMATSU Way 2. To anchor The KOMATSU Way, we will strengthen our Gemba capability through Kaizen activities in our routine work. Is management in line with societal 3. We will focus our efforts on brand management activities designed for us to demands? thoroughly understand customers’ Gemba and become indispensable for customers. → Always monitor (Supporting customers to achieve their ideal conditions) Code of Worldwide Business Conduct ● Rules that Komatsu and its management and employees must abide by as a member of the business society ● Statement to society as a “responsible corporate citizen” < Policies, Standards, Principles > ● 5 Principles of Compliance ● Earth Environmental Charter Corporate ● Declaration of Biodiversity ● Global Policy of Human Resources ● Occupational Safety and Health Policies ● Standards for Product Safety Citizenship ● Principles Governing Quality Assurance ● Basic Principles for Social Contributions ● Regional Policies, Standards by Countries, etc Komatsu’s CSR Themes 1.
